                 <div class="title-description prl ptm">
                  <h3 class="mtn mbxs">
                   <a class="link-stealth" href="/p/tell-ben-jerry-s-you-want-non-dairy-ice-cream-options">
                    Ben &amp; Jerry's to release non-dairy ice cream in 2016
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <p class="type-muted mtn">
                   After 28,000 people petitioned Ben &amp; Jerry's to add dairy-free ice cream to their flavor lineup, the iconic ice cream company announced their plan to release vegan-friendly ice cream in the US in 2016.
                   <a class="type-small" href="/p/tell-ben-jerry-s-you-want-non-dairy-ice-cream-options">
                    More
                   </a>
                  </p>
